<h1 _ngcontent-guc-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.contact (联系人)"> @ohos.contact (联系人) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供联系人管理能力，包括添加联系人、删除联系人、更新联系人等。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-guc-c106="" id="contactaddcontact10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">contact.addContact<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="contactaddcontact10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>addContact(context: Context, contact: Contact, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;): void</p>     <p>添加联系人。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.WRITE_CONTACTS</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Applications.ContactsData</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">应用上下文Context，Stage模型的应用Context定义见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-application-context">Context</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">contact</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-contact#contact">Contact</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">联系人信息。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。成功返回添加的联系人id；失败返回失败的错误码。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a <p>更新联系人。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7 开始支持，从API version 10 开始废弃，建议使用<a AsyncCallback&lt;Array&lt;Contact&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据电话号码查询联系人。使用callback异步回调。该接口仅返回联系人信息中的id、key、phoneNumbers属性。如果要查询联系人的所有信息，建议使用<a       <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>queryContactsByPhoneNumber(context: Context, phoneNumber: string, attrs: ContactAttributes, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Array&lt;Contact&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据电话号码和attrs查询联系人。使用callback异步回调。该接口仅返回联系人信息中的id、key、phoneNumbers属性。如果要查询联系人的所有信息，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-contact#contactquerycontact10-3">queryContact</a>接口，根据该接口返回的属性key查询。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.READ_CONTACTS</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Applications.ContactsData</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr> </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">phoneNumber</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">联系人的电话号码。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">attrs</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">回调函数。成功返回查询到的联系人对象数组；失败返回失败的错误码。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>queryContactsByPhoneNumber(phoneNumber: string, holder: Holder, attrs: ContactAttributes, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Array&lt;Contact&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据电话号码、holder和attrs查询联系人。使用callback异步回调。该接口仅返回联系人信息中的id、key、phoneNumbers属性。如果要查询联系人的所有信息，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-contact#contactquerycontact10-3">queryContact</a>接口，根据该接口返回的属性key查询。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7 开始支持，从API version 10 开始废弃，建议使用<a AsyncCallback&lt;Array&lt;Contact&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据email、holder和attrs查询联系人。使用callback异步回调。该接口仅返回联系人信息中的id、key、Emails属性。如果要查询联系人的所有信息，建议使用<a <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">联系人信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 782px;">     <h2 id="contactattributes" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">ContactAttributes<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="contactattributes" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>联系人属性列表，一般作为入参用来标识希望查询的联系人属性。</p>     <p>当传入为null时，默认查询全部属性。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Applications.ContactsData</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left"
